From all the testimonies on Facebook regarding the cashiers over charging, I  have absolutely no desire to visit this place. This person caught it but there was no reason something could be keyed in in such large quantities. There is no other produce on the receipt and it was done twice. To charge someone over $60. I understand human error. Keying in the wrong item so it ends up more than what it is. Or keying in the wrong quantity by mistake. But 44 of something that gets keyed in that isn't even being purchased. Twice. And everyone agreeing it's happened to them too. Shame on the cashier. And shame on the owner for going along w/it or not catching the multiple "mistakes".<//Text>

< review>
This is our go-to place for the care of our fur-babies.  This has also been the place we go to when we have to say goodbye to them.
In April of 2016 we had to put our beloved River to sleep. Regretfully, we had to put our sweet Kitty to sleep on September 5th.

We recommend them to everyone we know.

< review>
I've been coming to the GG Dog & Cat Hospital now for 9yrs. I have always received exceptional service by both the staff & all the doctors. The doctors truly care about the animals & are understanding when it comes to the high cost that can be associated with some of the care. Although they don't accept appts & can be very busy at times, the staff always do their best to be as professional & courteous as possible & it goes a long way! I recently moved out of the county but because of the amazing service provided I will go to no other vet/hospital & will always continue to go out of my way to come to the GG Dog & Cat Hospital. Keep up the amazing work Dr. Malo, Dr. Sanchez & the rest of the doctors & staff!< /review>

< review>
Great service and friendly staff! I do recommend some of the doctors there. The office is clean, and the staff will patiently take their time to answer all of your questions. Their management of paperwork is much better than some other places I have been to. Everything gets done in a timely manner, and they will keep you updated as to the progress of your pet.

However, beware of the bait-and-switch tactic: Sometimes, they'll give you a price over the phone, but when you get there, it's much more expensive! This was done to me twice. So, get the name of the person that quoted you.

Also, another tactic that was done by a doctor to me (I forgot her name) added another service to one of my dogs without even asking me! Extra cash for her I guess.

Overall, I do like and would recommend this place to my neighbors. Just beware of your pocket book. Some doctors are honest with pricing. But others can act like car  mechanics. Sorry, I'll have to get the names of the good ones later.<//review>

< review>
I have been going to GGDCH since about 2000. Have had three dogs live their lives as patients of Dr. Malo and now his son (UCD vet graduate, no less). I drive over 25 miles now to bring my current dogs to see them for everything because honestly I cannot trust other vets with my dogs. Darla, Chato both lived long lives under their care through many treatments, shots, etc. and now they care for my Chula, Petunia, and Tita. Their prices are very reasonable. For example, after I moved so far away, I tried another vet who tried to gouge me for a $3,000 treatment that Dr. malo said was unnecessary. They saved Chula from parvo as a puppy as well. So the drive and cost of gas is worth the professionalism, compassion, and care my pets receive from GGDCH. The wait can be a roll of the dice, but my dogs are worth it. Period.< /review>
